\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec}{A\+V\+Codec}} \mbox{\hyperlink{indeo3_8c_a5859f26ea702c33b837adef2f77ad0ec}{ff\+\_\+indeo3\+\_\+decoder}}
\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
This is a decoder for Intel Indeo Video v3. It is based on vector quantization, run-\/length coding and motion compensation. Known container formats\+: .avi and .mov Known F\+O\+U\+R\+C\+Cs\+: \textquotesingle{}I\+V31\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}I\+V32\textquotesingle{}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://wiki.multimedia.cx/index.php?title=Indeo_3}{\texttt{ http\+://wiki.\+multimedia.\+cx/index.\+php?title=\+Indeo\+\_\+3}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_acf8113e490f9e7b57465e65af9c0c75c}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx}} should have been set to a device of the specified type before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}!indeo3.c@{indeo3.c}}\index{indeo3.c@{indeo3.c}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{indeo3_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}\label{indeo3_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+S\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format for a decoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to a suitable frames context inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{doc_2examples_2qsvdec_8c_afe1023087c26d2d410c9cd7d491c8660}{get\+\_\+format()}} callback. The frames context must have been created on a device of the specified type.

When selecting this format for an encoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to the context which will be used for the input frames before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\

This format can be selected without any additional configuration -\/ no device or frames context is required. \\

A\+V\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+R\+O\+P\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+ED&Apply the maximum possible cropping, even if it requires setting the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}}\mbox{[}\mbox{]} entries to unaligned pointers. Passing unaligned data to F\+Fmpeg A\+PI is generally not allowed, and causes undefined behavior (such as crashes). You can pass unaligned data only to F\+Fmpeg A\+P\+Is that are explicitly documented to accept it. Use this flag only if you absolutely know what you are doing. \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} output\+\_\+plane (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_plane}{Plane}} $\ast$}]{plane,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{buf\+\_\+sel,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{ptrdiff\+\_\+t}]{dst\+\_\+pitch,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{dst\+\_\+height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Convert and output the current plane. All pixel values will be upsampled by shifting right by one bit.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em plane} & pointer to the descriptor of the plane being processed \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em buf\+\_\+sel} & indicates which frame buffer the input data stored in \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em dst} & pointer to the buffer receiving converted pixels \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em dst\+\_\+pitch} & pitch for moving to the next y line \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em dst\+\_\+height} & output plane height \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
